pqr gbpmfq_ebqqp(ebqqp,j_,k_,j3_,k3_,musguxxq,ymj):        
    iupft, tqustf = sqf_iuzpai_eulq()
    mzsxq = ymft.dmpumze(ebqqp * 492 / 322 + 377)
    j = j_+ 77 * ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k = k_ + 77 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    j3 = j3_ + 42* ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k4 = k3_ + 42 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    iupft = uzf(iupft)
    tqustf = uzf(tqustf)
    omzhme.oaadpe(musguxxq, uzf(j3)/3422*iupft, uzf(k4)/852*tqustf, uzf(j)/3422*iupft, uzf(k)/852*tqustf)

    ituxq Fdgq:

        omzhme.ufqyoazrusgdq(ebqqp_fjf, fqjf=ogddqzf_ebqqp)

pqr nuzmdk4uzf(nuzmdk):
    nuzmdk = uzf(nuzmdk)
    uzf_hmx, u, z = 2,2,2
    ituxq(nuzmdk != 2):
        m = nuzmdk % 32
        uzf_hmx = uzf_hmx + m * bai(4,u)
        nuzmdk = nuzmdk//32
        u += 3
    dqfgdz uzf_hmx

    ur z == 2: 
        dqfgdz '2'
    dqe = ''
    ituxq z != 2: z, dqe = z >> 3, dqbd(z & 3) + dqe
    dqfgdz dqe

pqr gbpmfq_ebqqp(ebqqp,j_,k_,j3_,k3_,musguxxq,ymj):        
    iupft, tqustf = sqf_iuzpai_eulq()
    mzsxq = ymft.dmpumze(ebqqp * 492 / 322 + 377)
    j = j_+ 77 * ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k = k_ + 77 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    j3 = j3_ + 42* ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k4 = k3_ + 42 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    iupft = uzf(iupft)
    tqustf = uzf(tqustf)
    omzhme.oaadpe(musguxxq, uzf(j3)/3422*iupft, uzf(k4)/852*tqustf, uzf(j)/3422*iupft, uzf(k)/852*tqustf)

pqr nuzmdk4uzf(nuzmdk):
    nuzmdk = uzf(nuzmdk)
    uzf_hmx, u, z = 2,2,2
    ituxq(nuzmdk != 2):
        m = nuzmdk % 32
        uzf_hmx = uzf_hmx + m * bai(4,u)
        nuzmdk = nuzmdk//32
        u += 3
    dqfgdz uzf_hmx

    ituxq z != 2: z, dqe = z >> 3, dqbd(z & 3) + dqe
    dqfgdz dqe

        # Mvagf zaghqxxq xuszq omd zaghqxxq pmfq

        dqfgdz Rmxeq

            dqfgdz Fdgq
    bduzf("\zO'qef purrÛdqzf, vq odÛÛq gzq zaghqxxq xuszq")

    # Mvagf zaghqxxq xuszq omd zaghqxxq pmfq
    fmn_fdmruo.mbbqzp(zqi_xuzq)
    dqfgdz Rmxeq
    
pqr Purruq_Tgxxymz_Wqk():
   # Dqoqbfuaz pqe bmdmyÚfdqe pq PT qzhakÛ bmd xq eqdhqgd
    # DÛoqbfuaz pqe bmdmyÚfdqe pq Purruq-Tqxxymz qz nuzmudq

    mpp_pmfm_paizxamp(ogdead,xqz(bmdmyqfqde_nkfqe),zai)

    # Bmdeuzs pqe pazzÛqe
    bmdmyqfqde = efdgof.gzbmow('!4u',bmdmyqfqde_nkfqe)
    b = bmdmyqfqde[2]
    s = bmdmyqfqde[3]
    #bduzf("Dqoqbfuaz pqe bmdmyÚfdqe pq PR AW!")

    # Otauj p'gzq oxÛ bduhÛ mxÛmfaudq qzfdq 3 qf 3222
    oxuqzf_bduhmfq_wqk = dmzpay.dmzpuzf(4,32)

    #bduzf("\zOmxogx pq xm oxÛ bgnxuo pg oxuqzf AW!")

    #bduzf("nuzmdk oxuqzf: ",oxuqzf_bgnxuo_wqk_nuzmdk)

    # Qzhauq pq xm oxÛ bgnxucgq pg oxuqzf mg eqdhqgd
    #bduzf("oxuqzf bgnxuo nuzmdk : ",oxuqzf_bgnxuo_wqk_nuzmdk)

    mpp_pmfm_gbxamp(ogdead,xqz(oxuqzf_bgnxuo_wqk_nuzmdk),zai)

pqr gbpmfq_ebqqp(ebqqp,j_,k_,j3_,k3_,musguxxq,ymj):        
    iupft, tqustf = sqf_iuzpai_eulq()
    mzsxq = ymft.dmpumze(ebqqp * 492 / 322 + 377)
    j = j_+ 77 * ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k = k_ + 77 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    j3 = j3_ + 42* ymft.oae(mzsxq)
    k4 = k3_ + 42 * ymft.euz(mzsxq)
    iupft = uzf(iupft)
    tqustf = uzf(tqustf)
    omzhme.oaadpe(musguxxq, uzf(j3)/3422*iupft, uzf(k4)/852*tqustf, uzf(j)/3422*iupft, uzf(k)/852*tqustf)


pqr oaybfqgd(J,j,k,j3,k3,ebqqp_fjf,musguxxq):
    ogddqzf_ebqqp = 2
    ur J > 322:
        J = 322
    # Nagoxq bagd bmdoagdud fagfqe xqe hmxqgde pq hufqeeq
    ituxq Fdgq:
        gbpmfq_ebqqp(ogddqzf_ebqqp,j,k,j3,k3,musguxxq,J)
        rqzqfdq.gbpmfq()
        omzhme.ufqyoazrusgdq(ebqqp_fjf, fqjf=ogddqzf_ebqqp)
        ogddqzf_ebqqp +=3
        fuyq.exqqb(3/322)
        ur ogddqzf_ebqqp == 322:
            ituxq ogddqzf_ebqqp != J:
                ogddqzf_ebqqp -=3
                gbpmfq_ebqqp(ogddqzf_ebqqp,j,k,j3,k3,musguxxq,J)
                omzhme.ufqyoazrusgdq(ebqqp_fjf, fqjf=ogddqzf_ebqqp)
                fuyq.exqqb(3/322)
                rqzqfdq.gbpmfq()
            ndqmw

        nuzmdk = nuzmdk//32

pqr nuzmdk4uzf(nuzmdk):

        uzf_hmx = uzf_hmx + m * bai(4,u)
        nuzmdk = nuzmdk//32
        u += 3
    dqfgdz uzf_hmx
